## Current Milestone

### M90 ÔÇö The Unproven-Assumption Doctrine (RISK-FIRST framing)

**Status:** DEFINED 2026-06-21 ÔÇö partition/plan DEFERRED. Supersedes/absorbs M89 (#36). Promoted from backlog #38. Version target: **minor** (new framework capability) ÔÇö 4.6.11 Ôćĺ 4.7.10 on complete.
**Autonomy note:** This milestone is RESEARCH-GATED and SELF-GOVERNING ÔÇö it must obey its own doctrine. No implementation approach is fixed at definition. The build sequence is **DISCUSS (researched, sourced approach) Ôćĺ intention-first PSEUDOCODE behavior-map (signed off) Ôćĺ PARTITION**. Scope split (factual-only / architectural-only / full / sequencing with M87/M89) is a DISCUSS OUTPUT, not a definition input.
**Branch:** continues on `m86-model-profiles` (no Expected-branch guard set; warn-and-proceed) ÔÇö a fresh `m90-unproven-assumption` branch is a partition-time decision, not now.

#### Origin
User, 2026-06-21, correcting M89's scope mid-flight (M89 PAUSED at verify after 8 cycles, plan-cleared code preserved at `ed03a8d`, 1824/0 tests, sound). M89 framed "guessing" as only FACTUAL ("do I know what the code/API currently SAYS?"). The user named the dangerous omission: the system also assumes an **APPROACH/architecture is correct without proof** ÔÇö "I'll fix it this way", "the existing code was written right, so I'll build on it" ÔÇö and **plows forward on the unproven approach**, repeatedly. Same pattern in three sagas the user named from "the last week across several projects":
- **binvoice** FB-modal whack-a-mole (+ PayPal premise) ÔÇö ~50ÔÇô100 turns, 7 `debug-cycle1` commits each a fix-for-the-prior-fix.
- **GSD-T M87** ÔÇö 7-cycle plan loop.
- **GSD-T M89** ÔÇö 8-cycle verify loop, each cycle a new "right fix" on a wrong deterministic-classifier premise.
Every time: guess an approach Ôćĺ plow forward Ôćĺ fail Ôćĺ guess another Ôćĺ repeat, instead of ONE step-back + research + re-architect. The re-scope trigger: M89's classifier recognized "external" via a hardcoded ~40-vendor list ÔÇö a frozen belief for an OPEN set; any out-of-list vendor (GitHub/Slack/OpenAI) silently routed internal Ôćĺ the exact silent-miss M89 exists to prevent. Memory: `feedback_unproven_assumption_stop_and_research`. User's directive: **"get this right the first time ÔÇö not build a patch and refactor later."**

#### Goal (the doctrine ÔÇö the real feature)
Any time the system relies on an UNPROVEN ASSUMPTION ÔÇö **FACTUAL** (do I know what the code/an API currently does?) OR **ARCHITECTURAL/APPROACH** (is THIS the right way to solve the problem? was the existing code written the right way so I can build on it?) ÔÇö it must **STOP, research how the problem has been solved successfully by others, RE-EXAMINE the premise, and only then proceed.** Plowing forward on an unverified approach is the deadly recurring pattern. "Don't act on belief; if not grounded in definitive knowledge or research, research first" ÔÇö applied to APPROACH, not just facts.

#### RISK-FIRST construction order (the distinct angle of this definition)
The build front-loads the **most-uncertain, most-likely-to-be-wrong** work so failure is cheap and early ÔÇö and so the milestone does not itself become the fourth multi-cycle saga. Ordered by descending risk (each gate must clear before the next is funded):

1. **R1 ÔÇö Does anyone know how to detect "an agent operating on an unproven ARCHITECTURAL premise" at all? (HIGHEST RISK ÔÇö unproven that a reliable mechanism exists.)** This is the new load-bearing capability with no in-house precedent. It is researched FIRST, in DISCUSS, before one line of design. If the research cannot surface a sound, sourced mechanism (LLM-as-judge / self-critique / reflection, retrieval-before-act, premise-re-examination on non-convergence), the milestone re-scopes DOWN to the factual slice rather than plowing forward ÔÇö the doctrine applied to itself. Failing here is cheap (a discuss spawn), not a 7-cycle execute loop.
2. **R2 ÔÇö The M89 vendor-list lesson, generalized and PROVEN on the open set (HIGH RISK ÔÇö the exact bug that paused M89).** The redesign of the recognition layer is risky precisely because it already failed once. Settle it early: the mechanical/regex layer recognizes ONLY CLOSED knowable sets (this repo's own files = internal); the LLM judges the open external world; uncertain Ôćĺ research. **Never hardcode a finite list for an open category.** A falsifiable known-answer test on out-of-list vendors is part of clearing this gate.
3. **R3 ÔÇö The non-convergence Ôćĺ re-examine-premise loop-hook (HIGH RISK ÔÇö must FIRE, not narrate).** The signature of an unproven premise is a debug/plan/verify loop producing variant-after-variant. The hook must HALT and re-examine the PREMISE/approach (research-then-rearchitect) instead of patching the next variant ÔÇö what should have fired ~5 cycles earlier in all three sagas. Risk is that it self-narrates a halt and proceeds anyway (the documented M89/binvoice failure: "I'll stop after this one" = no halt). Pairs with backlog #33's deterministic debug circuit-breaker (the firing teeth this borrows).
4. **R4 ÔÇö M89's factual slice, finished under this umbrella (LOWEST RISK ÔÇö code already exists at `ed03a8d`, sound).** Classifier + research + cite + ┬ž7 fail-closed gate becomes the FACTUAL slice. Redesigned per R2: delete the vendor list, regex-knows-only-own-paths, LLM-judges-the-rest. Lowest risk because the architecture is already validated; this is edit-in-place, not greenfield.
5. **R5 ÔÇö Contract + docs ripple (mechanical, last).** New/updated doctrine contract (absorbing `auto-research-contract.md`), CLAUDE-global Research Policy upgraded from advisory prose to the doctrine, requirements, README/GSD-T-README/help, package.json minor bump, lints.

Rationale for this order: R1 and R2 are where this milestone is most likely to be WRONG; proving or disproving them costs a discuss/pseudocode spawn. R4 is where it is most likely to be RIGHT (existing sound code). Front-loading R1ÔÇôR3 means any fatal premise surfaces before partition funds parallel execute domains ÔÇö failure is cheap and early.

#### Mandatory build sequence (the milestone obeys its own doctrine)
1. **DISCUSS** (multi-perspective, RESEARCH-GATED) ÔÇö explores the approach AND researches how others detect "an agent/system operating on an unproven assumption" (LLM-as-judge / self-critique / reflection, retrieval-before-act, premise-re-examination on non-convergence). **Must produce a researched, sourced approach** (citations) before plan is permitted. This settles the architecture AND the scope split. Resolves R1.
2. **Intention-first PSEUDOCODE behavior-map** (the M87/binvoice pattern, backlog #34): user supplies intentions, agent supplies VERIFIED mechanism, **zero code until signed off**. Locks behavior, resolving R2 and R3 at the behavior level before any implementation. The milestone is not partition-ready until this is signed off.
3. **THEN partition** ÔÇö and only then.

#### Falsifiable success criteria (measured per `feedback_measure_dont_claim`)
1. **SC-RESEARCH-GATE (process, falsifiable):** Plan is mechanically blocked until DISCUSS emits a sourced approach doc with Ôëą1 external citation per detection mechanism chosen. A plan attempt with no sourced approach FAILS. *(Falsifier: plan proceeds with zero citations.)*
2. **SC-NO-FINITE-LIST (the M89 lesson, falsifiable by known-answer test):** The recognition layer enumerates NO open category. A known-answer test feeds Ôëą10 out-of-any-prior-list external references (vendors/APIs/libraries never seen before, e.g. GitHub/Slack/OpenAI/a freshly-invented vendor name); each must route to LLM-judge-or-research, NONE silently classified internal. *(Falsifier: any unseen external reference classified internal without research.)*
3. **SC-LOOP-HOOK-FIRES (falsifiable, not narrated):** On a synthetic non-converging loop (3rd variant against the same computed symptom-signature), the hook deterministically HALTS the patch path and emits a premise-re-examination directive ÔÇö verified by ledger/exit-state, NOT by agent prose. A run that narrates "looping" but dispatches another point fix FAILS. *(Falsifier: 3rd same-signature variant dispatched without a halt.)*
4. **SC-ARCH-TRIGGER (the new load-bearing slice):** Given a task that builds on an existing approach without proof, the system raises an architectural-assumption trigger and requires "research how others solved this class of problem + re-examine premise" before proceeding ÔÇö demonstrated on a seeded case drawn from the three saga retros. *(Falsifier: builds on unproven approach with no trigger.)*
5. **SC-FACTUAL-PRESERVED:** M89's factual auto-research (classifier + research + cite + ┬ž7 fail-closed gate) remains green under the redesign ÔÇö test count Ôëą the `ed03a8d` baseline (1824/0), with the vendor list removed and replaced by regex-knows-own-paths + LLM-judges-rest. *(Falsifier: factual-slice regression vs. baseline.)*
6. **SC-FAIL-CLOSED:** When research is required but unavailable/inconclusive, the gate fails CLOSED (blocks, surfaces the unproven premise) ÔÇö never silently proceeds. *(Falsifier: any silent proceed on inconclusive research.)*
7. **SC-SELF-OBEDIENCE (meta):** The milestone's own artifacts show the doctrine applied to itself ÔÇö DISCUSS produced a sourced approach, PSEUDOCODE was signed off before code, and any mid-build non-convergence (Ôëą3 cycles same signature) triggered a documented premise re-examination rather than a variant patch. *(Falsifier: M90 itself runs a >2-cycle variant loop without a recorded premise step-back.)*

#### Sequencing notes
- **M87** is paused, plan-cleared, ready to execute ÔÇö resumes after M90's relevant slices land (its own plan loop was an instance of the pattern M90 fixes). **M89** code preserved at `ed03a8d`. M90 MAY re-scope M89 (folds its factual slice in as R4).
- **Scope is DELIBERATELY OPEN** ÔÇö the factual-only / architectural-only / full / M87-M89-sequencing split is a DISCUSS output, NOT fixed here. Likely ~3ÔÇô4 domains (factual auto-research [M89 redesigned] + architectural-assumption detection/research + non-convergenceÔćĺre-examine-premise loop-hook + contract/docs), multiple waves ÔÇö but that estimate is itself unproven and yields to the research.
- **Pairs with:** backlog #33 (debug circuit-breaker ÔÇö the loop-halt teeth R3 borrows), #34 (intention-first pseudocode ÔÇö the mandatory pre-partition gate), #31 (micro-pre-mortem). Out of scope: Red Team Realism gate (#39 ÔÇö separate, complementary).

#### Deferred (explicitly NOT this milestone yet)
Partition and plan. Next phase is DISCUSS (research-gated approach exploration), then intention-first PSEUDOCODE (signed off), then partition.

### M89 ÔÇö Auto-Research: deterministic external-info-gap resolution at every workflow phase  ÔĄ┤ SUPERSEDED-BY-M90

> **ÔĄ┤ SUPERSEDED/ABSORBED BY M90 2026-06-21.** M89's "external-fact auto-research" is the FACTUAL slice (M90 R4). Its built code (classifier + research + cite + ┬ž7 fail-closed gate, 1824/0 tests, sound) is PRESERVED at commit `ed03a8d` and folds into M90 edit-in-place ÔÇö redesigned per M90 R2 (delete the ~40-vendor list, regex-knows-only-own-paths, LLM-judges-the-rest). The rest of M89's definition below is retained for provenance.

**Status**: RE-PLANNED + CONFIRMED 2026-06-18 on the corrected premise (KNOWN-vs-GUESSED per-claim trigger). The prior plan run (b7fd3ea) BLOCKED on a TRANSIENT harness glitch (traceability `--domain` flag ignored Ôćĺ scanned all 425 repo tasks Ôćĺ exit 4 / gate-unparsed; pre-mortem verdict null in the envelope) ÔÇö NOT a plan defect. **Confirmation re-run with correct scope `--milestone M89`: BOTH M83 gates GREEN ÔÇö traceability exit 0 / 0 violations (24 tasks, 20 behavioral, headline M89-D1-T3 bound+tested); pre-mortem CLEARED (trustworthy verdict, 0 blocking findings) ÔÇö the cycle-2 CRITICALs stay DISSOLVED by the premise correction (verified on disk), not re-surfaced; the detection-can't-be-deterministic gap did NOT re-fire** (M89 no longer claims deterministic DETECT). EXECUTE-READY. 4 file-disjoint domains, 2 waves (W1 = D1 prove-or-kill classifier + D2 contract concurrent; W2 = D3 upper-phase + D4 worker-workflows gated on D1 A1). User-prioritized 2026-06-18; M87 paused for it. Execute next.
**Version target**: minor bump (new framework capability) ÔÇö 4.6.11 Ôćĺ 4.7.10 on complete
**Origin**: user, 2026-06-18. Direct evidence: binvoice S2-M5 (PayPal Invoicing v2) plan blocked on a pre-mortem where the agent had stated CONFIDENT GUESSES as known ÔÇö "PayPal mocked at the HTTP boundary", an assumed OAuth flow, an assumed invoice-TOTAL behavior ÔÇö none verified, all plausible. These recur every PayPal cycle because the agent ASSUMES the third-party contract instead of looking it up. Contrast M87 (0/7 web-resolvable ÔÇö pure introspection). The existing "Research Policy" in CLAUDE-global.md is advisory prose ("if in doubt, skip") ÔÇö LLM discretion that doesn't fire ([[feedback_deterministic_orchestration]]).

#### PREMISE CORRECTION (2026-06-18 ÔÇö the cycle-2 rethink)
Plan pre-mortem cycle-2 found 2 CRITICALs proving the original framing overclaimed: a "fully deterministic trigger that REPLACES the LLM 'should I research?' discretion" is impossible because **detecting that you need info is itself a judgment**. The user reframed it correctly: the trigger is not "did I notice a gap?" (passive, unnoticed gaps slip) but **"for every load-bearing claim ÔÇö is it KNOWN, or am I GUESSING?"** A guess is a claim ON THE PAGE, so it's inspectable (unlike an absent gap). M89 is therefore honestly scoped as: **deterministic CLASSIFY + cite-or-fail ENFORCE wrapped around an LLM-PROMPTED DETECT step** (the stage prompt requires the agent to tag its load-bearing claims, like the keep-or-supersede protocol ÔÇö best-effort, not magic). Determinism lives in steps 2ÔÇô3, not step 1.

#### The three guess-types (ANY triggers research/verification)
1. **Unknown** ÔÇö the agent lacks the fact.
2. **Assumed** ÔÇö asserting a shape/value never verified ("the create call returns a `url`" because it'd make sense, not because it was confirmed). Plausible Ôëá confirmed.
3. **Stale** ÔÇö knew it, but it's an external/time-varying fact with age (an API last seen months ago, a price, a model ID, a library signature). Was-true Ôëá is-true. **DEFAULT = FAIL TOWARD VERIFY:** any external/time-varying load-bearing fact without a FRESH cited source is treated as stale Ôćĺ search. Do NOT trust the agent's self-assessment of its own staleness ÔÇö that's another guess.

#### Goal
At every workflow phase (AND in direct conversation ÔÇö scope is both), for each load-bearing claim the agent tags KNOWN vs GUESSED (unknown/assumed/stale). A GUESSED claim is (a) CLASSIFIED internal-vs-external by a deterministic module, (b) external Ôćĺ a web-research `agent()` stage resolves it and CITES the fact + source URL into the artifact; internal Ôćĺ grep/Read; (c) the verify gate FAILS if a load-bearing external claim remains uncited (no silent guess). Result: confident-guess findings stop recurring because the fact is verified once and pinned.

#### The internal-vs-external classifier (deterministic, the load-bearing piece)
Given a GUESSED claim, it is EXTERNAL (Ôćĺ web) when it concerns a third-party API contract/endpoint/limit/return-shape/error-shape, a library/framework behavior or version, a platform/browser/runtime behavior, a standard/spec, or "current/latest." It is INTERNAL (Ôćĺ grep/Read/git, NEVER web) when it concerns this repo's own code/contracts/schema/ownership/sandbox/test architecture. The classifier routes by FEATURE CLASS (external-signal: third-party proper-noun OR an API/return-shape/limit/version/spec assertion about a system outside this repo ÔÇö so a proper-noun-LESS external guess like "max batch size the payments endpoint accepts" still routes external because it ASSERTS an external system's behavior unverified; internal-signal: repo path/symbol/"this repo/our/the existing"). Ambiguous Ôćĺ internal-first Ôćĺ grep Ôćĺ escalate to external only if grep returns nothing (owned by the wiring domains). Held-out generalization test guards against keyword-memorization.

#### Where it hooks in (every phase where it pays)
- **plan / pre-mortem** ÔÇö when a finding or task depends on an external fact (the S2-M5 case): research + cite into the contract/tasks BEFORE the gate re-runs, so the same finding doesn't re-fire.
- **partition / discuss / milestone** ÔÇö when decomposition or approach hinges on how an external system works.
- **execute** ÔÇö when a domain worker hits an unfamiliar API/library mid-build (don't guess ÔÇö look up + cite into the doc).
- **debug** ÔÇö when a failure's cause is external behavior (error message, API quirk, version regression); pairs with the #33 circuit-breaker (a debug cycle whose root is an external unknown should research, not patch-guess).
- **impact / quick / wave** ÔÇö same gap detection on their research-eligible steps.

#### Success Criteria (measurable)
- **SC1 (deterministic CLASSIFY):** `bin/gsd-t-research-gate.cjs` (house style ÔÇö JSON envelope) takes a GUESSED claim and returns `{class: internal|external, route: grep|web, reason}`, routing by FEATURE CLASS not memorized keywords. Pinned by the labeled corpus (13 seen: 7 M87Ôćĺinternal, 6 S2-M5Ôćĺ2-3 external) AND a disjoint HELD-OUT set (Ôëą6 novel, incl. a proper-noun-LESS external claim + a symbol-only internal). Bad input ('' / whitespace / non-string) Ôćĺ `{ok:false}`, never silent-internal.
- **SC2 (DETECT, LLM-prompted):** each eligible stage's prompt REQUIRES the agent to emit a structured **Stated Claims** list tagging every load-bearing claim KNOWN | GUESSED(unknown|assumed|stale) ÔÇö best-effort detection, the honest LLM step (like keep-or-supersede). The wiring iterates that list through the classifier. Staleness defaults to GUESSED for any external/time-varying fact lacking a fresh cited source (fail-toward-verify).
- **SC3 (research + cite):** a reusable research `agent()` stage (WebSearch/WebFetch) resolves an external guessed claim and writes a cited **Verified-Facts** block (fact + source URL + date) into the artifact. Uncited "fact" FAILS. Internal guess Ôćĺ grep/Read, never web.
- **SC4 (ENFORCE ÔÇö no silent guess):** the verify gate FAILS when a load-bearing claim tagged/detected external remains uncited. So the gate has something to check, the classifier writes a machine-readable external-claim marker into the artifact at classify time (a guess that proceeds uncited is caught even if the agent wrote nothing further).
- **SC5:** Advisory "Research Policy" prose in CLAUDE-global.md superseded by the known/guessed trigger (doc-ripple: CLAUDE-global.md + command files + `docs/requirements.md` entry per the Document Ripple gate).
- **SC6:** Applies in CONVERSATION too ÔÇö a standing directive (CLAUDE-global + memory `feedback_auto_research_external_gaps`): when answering the user about an external/time-varying fact, verify-or-flag before asserting (not a workflow gate; a habit rule).
- **SC7:** Regression ÔÇö full suite green; M71 runtime-native + M85 tier-policy lints pass; research `agent()` declares `model: "fable"` (bare literal, lint-clean).

#### Falsifiable Acceptance
- **A1 (load-bearing ÔÇö CLASSIFY generalizes):** classifier labels the seen 13 AND the disjoint held-out Ôëą6 matching hand-labels, deterministically ÔÇö including the proper-noun-LESS external claim (routes external by its unverified-external-assertion feature, not a keyword) and the symbol-only internal. "Passes seen, fails held-out" = FAILURE (kills keyword-memorization). Bad-input boundary asserted.
- **A2 (DETECT seam):** a fixture stage prompt emits a Stated Claims list; the wiring routes each through the classifier; a planted ASSUMED external claim ("the create call returns a `url`") and a planted STALE one (an aged API behavior) both route to research. A claim the agent failed to tag is an acknowledged best-effort miss (honest limit), NOT a silent pass for a TAGGED one.
- **A3 (research + cite, idempotent):** a planted external claim Ôćĺ Verified-Facts block with Ôëą1 source URL + date written to the artifact; a re-run with the fact ALREADY cited (exact normalized-claim-key) does NOT re-research; a DISTINCT external claim (PayPal-OAuth cited Ôëá PayPal-invoice-TOTAL) DOES research.
- **A4 (internal Ôćĺ no web):** a planted internal claim routes to grep/Read; the routing decision takes the grep branch and the research stage is never entered (the sandbox has no per-stage tool allowlist, so this is asserted on the routing decision + on the research stage being the SOLE web-capable prompt).
- **A5 (ENFORCE):** the dogfood e2e ÔÇö drive a fixture artifact with a planted external guess through classify Ôćĺ stubbed/offline research Ôćĺ cite Ôćĺ the verify gate: un-researched artifact FAILS (uncited external claim marker present), cited artifact PASSES. A state change in the artifact, not a source-grep.
- **A6:** Regression ÔÇö suite green + M71 + M85 lints pass; `docs/requirements.md` carries the M89 entry (doc-ripple).

#### Scope (GSD-T-native units)
- **~2 domains:** (1) **classifier + research stage** ÔÇö `bin/gsd-t-research-gate.cjs` (internal/external classifier + labeled-corpus test) + the reusable research `agent()` stage helper + Verified-Facts cite format; (2) **phase wiring + doc-ripple** ÔÇö hook the trigger into `gsd-t-phase.workflow.js` (plan/pre-mortem/partition/discuss/milestone) + execute/debug/quick/wave workflows at their research-eligible steps, replace the advisory Research Policy prose, new `.gsd-t/contracts/auto-research-contract.md` v1.0.0 STABLE.
- **2 waves.** W1 = classifier + the labeled-corpus A1 test (prove the internal/external call is reliable before wiring anything ÔÇö the risk-first lesson from M87). W2 = research stage + phase wiring, gated on A1.
- **Spawn count:** ~4ÔÇô6. **Rate-limit-window count:** 1.

#### Scope correction
Partition produced **4** file-disjoint domains (not the ~2 sketched): D1 classifier-core (prove-or-kill), D2 research-stage + contract + doc-ripple, D3 upper-phase+verify wiring (owns the dogfood e2e + the ENFORCE marker), D4 worker-workflow wiring. W1 = D1+D2; W2 = D3+D4 gated on D1 A1. The cycle-2 CRITICALs fold in as: the DETECT/Stated-Claims seam (SC2) + the external-claim marker so ENFORCE can fire (SC4/A5) ÔÇö both owned by the wiring domains.

#### Immediate dogfood
Once shipped, S2-M5's blocked plan re-runs WITH auto-research Ôćĺ the assumed PayPal facts (OAuth mint endpoint, invoice TOTAL limit, return-shape) get tagged GUESSED Ôćĺ researched Ôćĺ cited instead of recurring as pre-mortem findings. That's the acceptance demo (A5 is its deterministic offline proxy).

#### Deferred
Partition/plan (Next Up). M87 resumes after M89 completes.

### M87 ÔÇö Intention-First PseudoCode as Milestone Source-of-Truth (Risk-First)  ÔĆŞ PAUSED

> **ÔĆŞ PAUSED 2026-06-18 07:38 PDT** for M89 (auto-research), user-prioritized. Resume point: plan CLEARED + re-scoped (deterministic core; soft-ACs Ôćĺ M88), pre-execute. The 7-cycle plan loop is RESOLVED via the M87/M88 split + the cycle-7 structural finding (workflow runtime-testability) noted; NEXT action on resume = execute Wave 1 (guard-bridge-spike, prove-or-kill A1). No artifact changes needed to resume ÔÇö `git log` M87 commits end at 8711ef9 + c92a4e0. M89 ships first because its own evidence came partly from M87's loop (external-fact findings recurring) and from binvoice S2-M5 live.

**Status**: PLANNED + RE-SCOPED (deterministic-core split ÔÇö soft-ACs moved to M88; execute next) ÔÇö ÔĆŞ PAUSED for M89
**Version target**: minor bump (new framework feature) ÔÇö 4.6.11 Ôćĺ 4.7.10 on complete
**Origin**: Backlog #34 (added 2026-06-17), promoted 2026-06-17. From the binvoice `PseudoCode-PayPal.md` + `PseudoCode-Extension.md` exchange (session `35b4cbd7`). User reframe: this is a GENERATIVE tool, not a corrective one ÔÇö "work out all the details in an expressive way that made it clear what's going to happen and why and when." The user hand-wrote the Extension doc because GSD-T "wasn't understanding me"; this milestone bakes that hand-rolled rescue into the methodology so it's never needed as a rescue. Pairs with #31 (micro-pre-mortem) + #33 (debug circuit-breaker): #34 prevents the wrong build from starting ("do it right first"), the others reduce/halt damage during the build.

#### Goal
Make a two-altitude, intention-first PseudoCode document the signed-off source-of-truth at the FRONT of every milestone, and wire it MECHANICALLY downstream so partition/plan trace to it and verify checks the build against it ÔÇö a guard-map divergence is a FAILURE at contract severity. When the behavior map is confirmed in language before code, partitionÔćĺplanÔćĺexecuteÔćĺverify runs autonomously and delivers exactly what's expected ÔÇö eliminating the 50ÔÇô100-turn course-corrections measured twice this month.

#### Risk-First Framing (the distinct angle of this proposal)
The whole milestone's value rests on ONE uncertain claim: **that a prose `[RULE]` guard map can be turned into machine-checkable test assertions where divergence is a deterministic, non-vacuous FAILURE.** Everything else (template, two-altitude flow, sign-off gate, doc-ripple) is low-risk authoring/wiring work GSD-T has done many times. So this milestone is sequenced to PROVE or KILL the load-bearing claim before spending on the easy parts. If the guardÔćĺassertion bridge can't be made deterministic, we want to know on the first wave ÔÇö not after building the template and the sign-off UX around a hollow center.

**Risk-ranked work order (highest uncertainty first):**

1. **R1 ÔÇö Guard-map Ôćĺ assertion bridge (HIGHEST RISK, prove first).** Can a `[RULE]` line in a PseudoCode doc be parsed and bound to a verify-time check that FAILS on divergence and does NOT pass vacuously? This is novel ÔÇö the existing traceability-gate (`bin/gsd-t-traceability-gate.cjs`, M83) binds ACsÔćĺ(code path + named test) but never reads a prose spec doc or judges intention coverage. The new mechanism must: (a) enumerate every `[RULE]` from `PseudoCode-[Title].md`, (b) detect that each rule maps to Ôëą1 test assertion, (c) fail when a rule is unbacked OR contradicted (a divergence), at the same severity as a contract breach. The two binvoice exemplars are the fixture corpus ÔÇö if the bridge can't deterministically extract their guard maps and prove a planted divergence fails, the milestone's thesis is false. **Spike this in wave 1 against both exemplar docs before any template or command work.** Falsifiable kill-criterion: a `[RULE]`-map parser + verify check that, on a doctored exemplar with one rule deliberately violated by the "build," exits non-zero; and on the faithful build, exits zero ÔÇö both deterministically, zero LLM-judgment in the pass/fail decision (LLM may map, code must gate).

2. **R2 ÔÇö Traceability coupling: section-coverage + the competition-altitude shift (HIGH RISK, prove second).** Plan tasks must CITE the pseudocode section they implement (a section with no task = coverage gap, like journey-coverage); the M83 traceability-gate extends to require this citation. Risk: the existing gate is purely tasks.md-internal ÔÇö adding a cross-document coverage check (tasks.md Ôćö PseudoCode-[Title].md sections) is new surface and the place a second non-converging-Red-Team loop could ignite (cf. [[feedback_coverage_check_structural_not_substring]] ÔÇö coverage must parse structure, never substring-match). Also at risk: backlog #34 says competition (M82) shifts UP to the high-level-approach altitude when behavior is spec'd ÔÇö that interaction must be specified, not discovered at integrate. Prove the section-coverage check is structural and the competition-altitude rule is decided before building the authoring flow.

3. **R3 ÔÇö Keep-or-supersede guardrail + divergence provenance (MEDIUM RISK).** Before encoding ANY model inherited from shipped code, the agent MUST ask "keep this or supersede it?" per inherited model; every supersede emits a `ÔÜá Divergence` flag. This is the exact failure from the PayPal exchange (agent over-trusted the shipped S2-M4 stored-draft model; user: "We shouldn't be saving any draft of anything"). Medium risk because it's a prompt-protocol obligation, not a deterministic gate ÔÇö its reliability is bounded by how forcing we can make the question. Decide whether the divergence count is itself a checkable artifact (it should feed R1's map).

4. **R4 ÔÇö Two-altitude milestone flow + sign-off gate (LOW RISK, build last).** High-level pseudocode first (approach: what/why/when, actors, one-breath summary) Ôćĺ user signs off the APPROACH Ôćĺ detailed decomposition to `PseudoCode-[Title].md` at PayPal-doc granularity Ôćĺ milestone is NOT "DEFINED" until the detailed doc is signed off. Default-ON for all milestones (greenfield benefits most ÔÇö no shipped code to ground in, so the pseudocode IS the spec); skippable per-milestone for trivial work, skip is a LOGGED decision not silent ([[feedback_no_silent_degradation]]). Low risk: this is `/gsd-t-milestone` + its phase-workflow flow plus a sign-off checkpoint ÔÇö known GSD-T patterns.

5. **R5 ÔÇö Template + doc-ripple integration (LOWEST RISK, build last).** Ship `templates/PseudoCode-spec.md` (intention/mechanism/guard-map/divergence/appendix skeleton + two-altitude structure), anchored to the binvoice exemplars not a blank page. Add `PseudoCode-[Title].md` to the Living Documents ripple set: `templates/CLAUDE-global.md` Living Documents table (line ~60), Pre-Commit Gate, `commands/gsd-t-doc-ripple.md` ÔÇö so when code/contract/schema changes mid-milestone, the pseudocode doc updates in the same pass and stays the truth, not a stale snapshot.

#### Document format (observed, from the two binvoice exemplars)
Each section pairs a `> **Intention ({Author}, {date}).**` prose block (the WHY/directive ÔÇö dated + attributed for durable provenance) ABOVE a fenced pseudocode block (the verified HOW), plus: a "one call in one breath" summary table, a guard-enumeration map rendering every invariant as a one-line `[RULE]`, explicit `ÔÜá Divergence` flags wherever a new intention supersedes shipped code, and a raw-pseudocode appendix with intention prose stripped (the build's quick-reference). Grounds in EXISTING contracts/schema rather than inventing field names; defers concrete identifiers to plan-time-against-real-schema. Doc prose is INTENTION (the user's), never agent reasoning ÔÇö agent reasoning stays out of the doc.

**Naming convention.** Instances are `PseudoCode-[Title].md` where `[Title]` names what the doc REPRESENTS (its subject), NOT a milestone id ÔÇö e.g. `PseudoCode-PayPal.md`, `PseudoCode-Extension.md` (both binvoice exemplars coexist today). A project holds MANY pseudocode docs, and a single milestone may produce several (one per coherent subject/subsystem). Only `templates/PseudoCode-spec.md` keeps the `-spec` name ÔÇö it is the shipped blank skeleton (the mold), not an instance.

#### Success Criteria (measurable ÔÇö TRIMMED to the deterministic core after the cycle-4 split; the soft-AC halves moved to M88, see "Descoped to M88" below)
- **SC1 (load-bearing):** A new mechanism extracts the `[RULE]` guard map from `PseudoCode-[Title].md` and, at verify, gates the build against it ÔÇö a divergence (unbacked or contradicted rule) FAILS at contract-breach severity. The pass/fail decision is deterministic code, not LLM judgment. _(Scope: the gate's DISCRIMINATION of a buildÔćĺrule map ÔÇö faithful map Ôćĺ 0, doctored map Ôćĺ non-zero. The map-DERIVATION path moves to M88.)_
- **SC2:** Plan tasks cite the pseudocode section they implement; a section with zero implementing tasks is reported as a coverage gap (structural parse, not substring). The M83 traceability-gate is extended, not replaced. **Plus the cycle-4 gate-scoping fix:** `--milestone M87` scopes to EXACTLY the four M87 domains (which are subject-named, no `m87` prefix), never falling back to all historical domains.
- **SC3 (FLOW/protocol only ÔÇö the deterministic sign-off GATE is M88):** `/gsd-t-milestone` runs the two-altitude flow: high-level approach sign-off precedes detailed-doc generation; default-ON; skip is logged. The flow + keep-or-supersede PROMPT ship here as prose/protocol. The machine-checkable "milestone is not DEFINED until signed off" GATE (a concrete sign-off marker + a code-readable `isDefined(milestone)` predicate) moves to M88 ÔÇö no such state artifact exists in the codebase today.
- **SC5:** `PseudoCode-[Title].md` is in the Living Documents ripple set across all four reference points (Living Documents table, Pre-Commit Gate, doc-ripple command, project CLAUDE.md) ÔÇö kept identical (ripple intact).
- **SC6:** `templates/PseudoCode-spec.md` ships, structurally matching the binvoice exemplars (both altitudes + all five section elements present).
- **SC7 (folded mechanical finding ÔÇö derived-id stability):** D1's faithful-map keyset is generated PROGRAMMATICALLY from the parser's derived ids at test setup (or via a documented regen script), not hand-maintained ÔÇö so a fixture re-copy reflows doc ids AND map keyset together.

#### Descoped to M88 (moved out of M87 at the cycle-4 split ÔÇö resist deterministic gating at current scope)
The user split M87 after 4 plan-phase pre-mortem cycles (8Ôćĺ5Ôćĺ2Ôćĺ6 findings). These four pieces each set the same deterministic-gate bar the M87 core meets, but cannot meet it as-scoped without their own design ÔÇö so they become follow-up milestone **M88** (backlog #35), which DEPENDS on M87 (the guard-bridge gate + the two-altitude flow must exist first):
- **A3 deterministic sign-off STATE/GATE** ÔÇö there is NO milestone-state artifact today ("DEFINED" is prose an LLM writes in this file). M88 designs a concrete sign-off marker + a code-readable `isDefined(milestone)` predicate. (M87 still ships the two-altitude FLOW + keep-or-supersede PROMPT as prose/protocol.)
- **A1 map-GENERATION path** ÔÇö A1's doctored fixture differs only in the LLM-produced `--map` JSON, so the gate's discrimination of a doctored MAP is proven; the map-DERIVATION path (build Ôćĺ `[RULE]`-backing map) is untested. M88 designs the mechanical map-generation seam + its end-to-end test.
- **A5 verify-triad consumption** ÔÇö must be a DETERMINISTIC seam-check (assert the qa/red-team prompts contain the structured directive to ingest the rule set + a unit test feeding guard-map JSON), NOT a live triad run. M88 gives it that design.
- **SC4 divergence grammar** ÔÇö the deterministic `parseDivergence()`/`formatDivergence()` grammar round-trip moves to M88. The "agent ASKS keep-or-supersede" half is an inherent prose PROTOCOL (acknowledged not-a-gate) and ships in M87's D3 prompt.

#### Falsifiable Acceptance (TRIMMED ÔÇö every remaining AC is deterministically gateable; A3/A5/SC4-deterministic + the A1-map-gen AC moved to M88, see "Descoped to M88")
- **A1 (kills the milestone if it fails):** Take a faithful build of one binvoice exemplar and a doctored variant with exactly one `[RULE]` deliberately violated **in the buildÔćĺrule MAP** (the doc stays byte-identical; doctoring flips a map entry). The new verify check exits ZERO on the faithful map and NON-ZERO on the doctored one, deterministically, with the violated rule named. If this can't be built deterministically, R1 is unsatisfiable and the milestone halts for re-scoping (escalate, don't paper over ÔÇö [[feedback_coverage_check_structural_not_substring]]). _(The map-GENERATION path ÔÇö how the build PRODUCES that map ÔÇö is M88; A1 proves the gate's DISCRIMINATION.)_
- **A2:** A test feeds a tasks.md that omits a task for one pseudocode section; the extended traceability-gate reports that section as an uncovered gap (structural, path-as-path ÔÇö passes the binvoice exemplar corpus, fails the planted gap). **Plus gate-scoping (cycle-4 MEDIUM):** `test/m87-gate-milestone-scoping.test.js` asserts `--milestone M87` scopes to EXACTLY the four M87 domains, zero historical.
- **A4:** A drift lint (M71-family pattern) asserts `PseudoCode-[Title].md` appears in ALL FOUR ripple reference points; removing it from any one FAILS the lint (mandatory negative test).
- **A6 (regression ÔÇö salvaged from sibling proposal):** Full suite stays green (baseline 1603/1607); the **M71 runtime-native lint** passes (any workflow edit stays sandbox-clean ÔÇö no `require`/`fs`/`process`) and the **M85 tier-policy lint** passes. Any workflow `model:` literal added stays policy-conformant.
- **A7 (folded mechanical finding ÔÇö derived-id stability):** D1's faithful map keyset is generated programmatically from the parser's derived ids at test setup; a re-copied fixture that reflows ids keeps the map keyset == the derived id set with no hand-edit (the M87-D1-T3 keyset-equality assertion proves it).

_(Moved to M88: **A3** machine-checkable sign-off STATE/predicate; **A5** triad-consumption deterministic seam-check; the **A1 map-GENERATION** end-to-end test; the **SC4 `parseDivergence()`/`formatDivergence()`** grammar round-trip. Each needs its own design ÔÇö see "Descoped to M88" and backlog #35.)_

#### Scope (GSD-T-native units ÔÇö partitioned into 4 file-disjoint domains; TRIMMED to the deterministic core)
- **4 domains:** **D1 guard-bridge-spike** ÔÇö the `[RULE]`Ôćĺassertion mechanism (new `bin/gsd-t-guard-map.cjs`) + the A1 falsifiable harness + verify wiring (R1, the load-bearing half); **D2 traceability-section-coverage** ÔÇö extends `bin/gsd-t-traceability-gate.cjs` for section-citation coverage + the folded cycle-4 **gate-scoping** fix (`--milestone M87` scopes to exactly the 4 subject-named M87 domains) (R2); **D3 milestone-two-altitude-flow** ÔÇö `/gsd-t-milestone` + phase-workflow (`templates/workflows/gsd-t-phase.workflow.js`, phase `"milestone"`) ship the two-altitude FLOW + keep-or-supersede PROMPT as prose/protocol (R3+R4); the deterministic sign-off GATE (A3) is descoped to M88; **D4 template-docripple-contract** ÔÇö `templates/PseudoCode-spec.md`, Living Documents ripple integration, `.gsd-t/contracts/pseudocode-source-of-truth-contract.md` v1.1.4 STABLE (R5).
- **2 waves.** Wave 1 = the D1 R1 spike against both binvoice exemplars (PROVE the bridge before anything downstream). Wave 2 = D2/D3/D4, built only after D1 passes A1. D3 ships the FLOW/protocol, NOT the deterministic sign-off gate (that gate moves to M88).
- **Spawn count:** ~6ÔÇô9 (3 domain workers ├Ś ~2 + the R1 spike + verify triad).
- **Rate-limit-window count:** 1.

#### File ownership note (carried forward to partition ÔÇö file-disjointness invariant)
Partition MUST validate domain file-disjointness via `gsd-t parallel --dry-run` and confirm any workflow edits stay within the M71 sandbox. The shared touch surfaces (`commands/gsd-t-verify.md`, `bin/gsd-t.js` CLI dispatch, `templates/CLAUDE-global.md`) are integrate-time seams, NOT parallel-written. No file is assigned to two domains.

#### Deferred (explicitly NOT this milestone)
Partition and plan (the Next Up successors). The high-level approach altitude of THIS milestone's own pseudocode is itself a candidate first user of the feature once R1 proves out ÔÇö but bootstrapping is deferred to avoid a chicken-and-egg dependency.

#### Why risk-first wins here
The cheap-and-early-failure principle: R1 is the only part that could be impossible, and it's testable against two real exemplar docs we already have. Building the template, the sign-off UX, and the doc-ripple wiring first would sink the bulk of the spend into scaffolding around an unproven center ÔÇö and if the guardÔćĺassertion bridge then proves un-deterministic (the known non-converging-Red-Team trap for coverage checks), all of it is rework. Proving R1 in wave 1 means a kill decision costs one spike, not a milestone.

**Competition outcome**: winner = proposal A of 3 (the **risk-first** sequencing) ÔÇö chosen over the fastest-time-to-value (beachhead) and the strict-dependency-order (lexicon-first topological) framings. Salvaged into A1/A2 the structural-coverage and exemplar-corpus emphasis; salvaged the explicit M71/M85 lint regression bar as A6; salvaged the partition file-disjointness validation note. The two siblings' Wave-0-contract-first and beachhead-authoring-first orderings were NOT folded ÔÇö they conflict with risk-first's load-bearing-claim-first sequencing (proving R1 before scaffolding).

### M84 ÔÇö Auto-Competition (workflow self-decides whether to run a competition) ÔÇö **COMPLETED at v4.3.10 (2026-06-05 20:42 PDT)**

**Status: COMPLETED ÔÇö VERIFIED.** Single domain (auto-competition probe + opt-inÔćĺautomatic conversion), built in-session. Origin: user, watching M82 competition stay opt-in: *"I do not want this to be opt-in. I want the workflow to determine when it's optimal to create a competition ÔÇö three producers with a judge."* And the economic case (user): a better artifact produced upstream makes every downstream phase (pre-mortem, execute, verify) cheaper + more likely to pass first time, so the expected savings exceed the ~3├Ś upstream cost ÔÇö opt-in just means forgetting to use the thing that lowers total cost.

**Built.** Converted M82 competition from opt-in (`--competition N`) to AUTOMATIC in `templates/workflows/gsd-t-phase.workflow.js`: a **solution-space probe** runs at the start of each eligible phase (partition/milestone/discuss/design-decompose), after brief, before producing, and self-decides compete (3 producers + judge) vs single-draft. (a) **Probe on OPUS, not haiku** ÔÇö deciding "Ôëą2 genuinely different viable approaches?" is high-level reasoning that gates the whole 3├Ś competition; a weak probe forfeits the feature (user caught this: *"Is Haiku smart enough to make this a judgment?"* ÔÇö no). (b) **Biased toward competing** ÔÇö uncertain Ôćĺ compete; probe failure Ôćĺ compete (fail-toward-options). (c) **Partition**: opus probe makes the pre-produce compete/skip call, the objective file-disjointness oracle still JUDGES the candidates. (d) **Phase-aware producer angles** (`ANGLES_BY_PHASE`) so a discuss/milestone/design producer isn't handed a partition-framed directive (Red Team MEDIUM). (e) **Overrides** (rarely needed): `competition: N` (2-5) force N, `competition: 0`/`noCompetition` force off, unset = auto; unparseable override warns + falls back to auto. (f) `meta.phases` now declares all 7 stages (also fixes the M83 cosmetic Plan-Hardening omission).

**Verification (real-sandbox + triad).**
- **Real-sandbox probe proof:** the opus probe ran through the actual Workflow sandbox and discriminated correctly ÔÇö WIDE scenario (real-time collaborative editor, multiple architectures) Ôćĺ **compete=true, 3 approaches named** (CRDT-vs-OT / sync-authority / deployment-topology); NARROW scenario (bump copyright year, one file) Ôćĺ **compete=false** (*"exactly one correct outcome"*). Validates the user's instinct: the probe needs Opus-level reasoning, and it discriminates rather than blanket-competing.
- **Red Team (adversarial Workflow, Opus, fresh context): GRUDGING-PASS** ÔÇö no CRITICAL/HIGH. Verified clean: state-wiring (let-decls set before consumers, no read-before-set), override logic (force-off/force-N/clamp/unset-Ôćĺ-probe all correct), eligibility (plan/impact/prd/doc-ripple/execute can NEVER compete), probe-failure (fail-toward-compete, can't crash/loop), cost-bound (1 probe + ÔëĄ5 producers + ÔëĄ2 judge + finalize + revalidate, no runaway), runtime-native, and no plan-hardening regression. Fixed the 1 MEDIUM (phase-aware angles ÔÇö the latent M82 defect that now mattered because competition is the default path) + 3 LOWs (misleading partition-oracle comment, unparseable-arg warning, empty "Phase" stage on the competition path).
- **QA:** suite **1372 pass / 0 fail / 4 skip**; M71 runtime-native lint passes.

**Domain table:**

| Domain | Status | Tasks | Completed |
|--------|--------|-------|-----------|
| m84-auto-competition | verified | ÔÇö | ÔÇö |

**Versioning:** minor bump 4.2.10 Ôćĺ 4.3.10 (changed behavior ÔÇö competition now automatic; additive overrides). Contract `competition-mode-contract.md` Ôćĺ v2.0.0. Tagged v4.3.10.

### M83 ÔÇö Left-Shifted Plan Hardening (acceptance-traceability gate + adversarial pre-mortem) ÔÇö **COMPLETED at v4.2.10 (2026-06-05 19:29 PDT)**

**Status: COMPLETED ÔÇö VERIFIED.** 2 file-disjoint domains (D1 deterministic traceability gate ┬Ě D2 adversarial pre-mortem protocol + plan-workflow wiring), built in-session. Origin: review of the NiceNote 9-milestone build, where the triad caught real bugs but LATE ÔÇö M5's headline capability (100MB+ chunked read) shipped as DEAD CODE and burned 4 verify cycles. User's diagnosis: the failure is upstream in plan/scope; user's proposal: an adversarial risk-assessment agent at plan time. This milestone left-shifts failure detection from verify to plan.

**Goal (delivered).** Two blocking gates in the `plan` phase, run after the plan agent writes tasks.md and BEFORE execute: (1) deterministic **acceptance-traceability gate** ÔÇö every behavioral task binds its ACs to a code path + a killing test; the headline must be impl+test; (2) adversarial **pre-mortem** ÔÇö opus, fresh-context, predicts edge-case/dead-deliverable/NFR failures, each Ôćĺ a required test. The temporal dual of the Red Team (attack the design at plan, not just code at verify). The pre-mortem makes the post-mortem cheap.

**Built.** (a) `bin/gsd-t-traceability-gate.cjs` ÔÇö parses `.gsd-t/domains/*/tasks.md`, emits `{ok,exitCode,violations}`; exit 4 blocks execute. Emphasis-stripped + colon-agnostic field detection; AC-anchored task detection (descriptive headings not dropped); test-check tied to Test/Files/AC fields; pytest conventions preserved; zero deps, never throws, pure. Dispatched as `gsd-t traceability-gate`; project + global bin tools. (b) `templates/prompts/pre-mortem-subagent.md` ÔÇö the adversarial PLAN protocol (verdict BLOCK/CLEARED; every finding Ôćĺ a requiredTest; advisory notes forbidden). (c) plan-phase wiring in `gsd-t-phase.workflow.js` ÔÇö gate (fail-closed) Ôćĺ short-circuit on block Ôćĺ pre-mortem; runtime-native (M71 lint passes). (d) contract `.gsd-t/contracts/plan-hardening-contract.md` v1.0.0 (6 invariants). (e) plan objective strengthened to require traceable tasks up front. (f) doc-ripple: gsd-t-plan.md, README, gsd-t-help, CLAUDE-global (+ live ~/.claude/CLAUDE.md), project CLAUDE.md (protocols + brains lists), package.json minor bump.

**Verification (orthogonal triad + self-test against the origin failure).**
- **Self-test (the milestone's reason to exist):** the gate run against the actual NiceNote M5 dead-code plan (headline AC-6, chunked read, no test) Ôćĺ **FAIL exit 4** with `headline-without-test` ÔÇö caught at plan time, the failure that previously took 4 verify cycles.
- **Red Team (adversarial Workflow, Opus, fresh context):** FAILed first pass ÔÇö **1 CRITICAL** (colon-inside-bold `**Acceptance criteria:**` markdown ÔÇö the exact form the contract tells authors to write ÔÇö defeated ALL field detection, silently passing the literal M5 dead-code plan) + 2 HIGH (descriptive headings dropped; `**Headline:** true` never registered) + 2 MEDIUM (runner word in an unrelated field cleared the test check; gate-unparsed fail-open). All 5 fixed (emphasis-strip + colon-agnostic regexes, AC-anchored parsing, field-tied test check, fail-closed gate).
- **Re-validation Red Team:** all 5 confirmed fixed ÔÇö but found a **regression the CRITICAL fix introduced** (underscore-stripping in `_bare` broke pytest `test_*.py`/`*_test.py` paths Ôćĺ false-FAIL valid Python plans, HIGH). Fixed via `_barePath`/`fieldValueRaw` (preserve underscores for value-level scans, strip emphasis only for label detection).
- **Final re-validation:** GRUDGING-PASS ÔÇö 14/14 checks confirmed by execution, no new HIGH/CRITICAL. One INFO LOW (a non-headline task whose only Files entry is named like a test passes) judged pre-existing + self-consistent + caught for headlines; left as documented behavior.
- **QA:** suite **1372 pass / 0 fail / 4 skip** (+15 M83 tests); M71 runtime-native lint passes; **real-sandbox acceptance gate passed** (the traceability gate fires through the actual Workflow sandbox and blocks the bad plan ÔÇö `via=local, blockedAsExpected=true`).

### M82 ÔÇö Competition Mode (generate-and-judge for upstream wide-solution-space phases) ÔÇö **COMPLETED at v4.1.10 (2026-06-05 17:49 PDT)**

**Status: COMPLETED ÔÇö VERIFIED.** 2 file-disjoint domains (D1 judge engine + workflow arm ┬Ě D2 contract + flags + doc-ripple), built in-session. Origin: brainstorm 2026-06-05 grounded in 2 deep-research runs (tasks `wkcnmqw8u` best-of-N/judge/debate + `wt4z2eqcp` synthesis-vs-pick-one/MoA/Frankenstein). Full spec in `.gsd-t/backlog.md` #26.

**Goal (delivered).** Opt-in `competition: N` on **upstream, pre-contract, wide-solution-space phases** (partition / milestone / discuss / design-decompose): fan out N parallel candidate-producers Ôćĺ a **judge stage** Ôćĺ winner. The *generative dual* of the orthogonal validation triad (adversarial). **Watershed rule: generate-and-judge ABOVE the contract; attack-and-filter BELOW it.** Never touches execute/plan/verify/integrate.

**Evidence base (citable, verified).** Best-of-N coverage scales log-linearly but is **judge-bounded** (Brown et al. arXiv 2407.21787; 3-vote) Ôçĺ the judge IS the feature. Synthesis beats pick-one on loosely-coupled tasks (MoA arXiv 2406.04692; 3-0) but NOT unconditionally (Frankenstein real). Frankenstein mechanism = candidate quality variance; **Self-MoA > Mixed-MoA** (arXiv 2502.00674; 3-0) Ôçĺ N samples of one strong model. Debate doesn't beat sampling+judge Ôçĺ skip it. Optimal N<10 Ôçĺ default off, cap 5.

**Built.** (a) `bin/gsd-t-competition-judge.cjs` ÔÇö the selection oracle: `--kind partition` (objective, scores candidate decompositions via the SAME `bin/gsd-t-file-disjointness.cjs` oracle the dispatcher uses ÔÇö a calculator, not an LLM critic; touch-path normalization) + `--kind generic` (deterministic rubric selector). Zero deps, never throws, pure. Dispatched as `gsd-t competition-judge`; added to project + global bin tools. (b) `templates/workflows/gsd-t-phase.workflow.js` ÔÇö the competition arm: `competition: N` (clamp 2ÔÇô5, default off) on eligible phases Ôćĺ `parallel()` of N Self-MoA producers (one strong model, prompt-angle diversity) Ôćĺ judge stage Ôćĺ finalizer (pick-one-at-thesis + union-at-line-item) Ôćĺ partition re-validates the graft and BLOCKS on a reintroduced overlap. Runtime-native (M71 lint passes). (c) `.gsd-t/contracts/competition-mode-contract.md` v1.0.0 STABLE (6 invariants). (d) `--competition N` flag + docs on `gsd-t-partition.md` / `gsd-t-milestone.md` / `gsd-t-design-decompose.md`. (e) doc-ripple: README, gsd-t-help, CLAUDE-global (+ live `~/.claude/CLAUDE.md`), project CLAUDE.md, package.json minor bump.

**Verification (orthogonal triad + measured SCs).**
- **SC#1 (headline, MEASURED on M82's own partition):** competition with 3 candidate partitions Ôćĺ winner `B-by-layer` with **3 parallel groups** (judge-engine Ôłą workflow-arm Ôłą contract-and-flags, file-disjoint) vs the **N=1 baseline's 1** parallel group Ôćĺ **3├Ś measured parallelism**, strictly better. The deliberately-overlapping candidate (`C-overlap-trap`, shared `bin/gsd-t.js`) was correctly **disqualified** (`valid:false`) ÔÇö a naive "more domains = better" judge would have picked it.
- **SC#2 (no Frankenstein):** invalid candidates never selected (HIGH-1 fix: all-invalid Ôćĺ hard-fail, not `candidates[0]`); finalized partition re-validated via the oracle, blocks on salvage overlap (HIGH-2 fix).
- **SC#3 (position-bias):** objective judge order-invariant (100%, reverse-order probe Ôćĺ same winner).
- **SC#4 (cost):** bounded by construction (N producers + judge + finalizer, no loops).
- **Red Team (adversarial Workflow, Opus, fresh context):** FAILed first pass ÔÇö 3 HIGH (invalid-partition fallback to candidates[0]; finalizer never re-validated; subjective judge claimed-but-not-shuffled) + 2 MEDIUM (judge() threw on null candidate; unquoted projectDir + unescaped backticks). All 5 fixed; **re-validation Red Team GRUDGING-PASS** (all confirmed fixed by reading logic + executing scenarios, no new HIGH/CRITICAL). 2 LOW from recheck also closed (finalizedDomains now schema-required + absence blocks; tiebreak wording corrected). Re-confirms the orthogonal-validation contract: a fresh-context Workflow Red Team caught what the in-context build missed.
- **QA:** suite **1357 pass / 0 fail / 4 skip** (+6 M82 tests); M71 runtime-native lint passes; **real-sandbox acceptance gate passed** (judge integration ran end-to-end in the actual Workflow sandbox ÔÇö proof v2: via=local, winner=B-by-layer, pass=true; the v1 proof caught a real envelope-propagation bug that lint+node --check could not, then fixed).

**Domain table:**

|--------|--------|-------|-----------|

### M67 ÔÇö Scan Deep Document Phase ÔÇö **COMPLETED at v4.0.14 (2026-05-29 22:06 PDT)**

**Status: COMPLETED ÔÇö VERIFIED. Single domain `m67-d1-scan-document-stage`. Origin: user asked "does scan now do a more thorough document job on ALL the documents it produces?" ÔÇö answer was NO. M66 made the tech-debt register deep but left living-document cross-population as a non-deterministic "lead agent follow-on" (effectively dropped) ÔÇö a regression vs the old prose scan's Step 5. M67 adds a deterministic `Document` phase between Synthesis and Render: one agent PER DOCUMENT fans out (parallel) from the same slices + verified findings, producing the full living-doc set (`docs/architecture.md`, `docs/workflows.md`, `docs/infrastructure.md`, `docs/requirements.md`, `README.md` ÔÇö merge-not-overwrite) + the five `.gsd-t/scan/*.md` dimension files (architecture/security/quality/business-rules/contract-drift) in the renderer's parsed formats. Covers everything old Step 5 did and goes deeper (component map + a user journey per feature-domain slice). Synthesis no longer writes the dimension files (moved to the doc stage). Red Team FAILed (2 HIGH + 1 LOW); 1 fix cycle Ôćĺ GRUDGING-PASS. Zero regressions (1267/0/4 throughout). Patch bump 4.0.13 Ôćĺ 4.0.14. Commits 82a2f9c (build) Ôćĺ bec1556 (fix HIGH-1 doc-snapshot data-loss backstop + HIGH-2 grand-total-as-table-row double-count fix + LOW drop -f) Ôćĺ gitignore .doc-backup.**

**Verify findings & fixes (Red Team):** HIGH-1 ÔÇö living-doc agents "merge not overwrite" was prose-only and a dirty tree doesn't halt scan Ôćĺ uncommitted user edits could be clobbered unrecoverably (Destructive Action Guard). Fix: deterministic snapshot of all 5 living docs to `.gsd-t/scan/.doc-backup/` BEFORE the fan-out (mirrors the register's deterministic archive); merge note mandates Edit-not-Write on existing files. HIGH-2 ÔÇö arch prompt mandated a bare `N files (~N LOC)` grand-total line + a per-dir Structure section Ôćĺ collector's additive regex double-counts filesScanned. Fix: grand total is now a `| Grand Total | N files | LOC |` table row that the parser short-circuits on (empirically verified: table row + per-dir lines Ôćĺ filesScanned=1809 not 1919). LOW ÔÇö dropped `-f` from git add (force-added .DS_Store) + `:!.doc-backup` exclusion + gitignore entry. Re-verify GRUDGING-PASS, all empirically confirmed.

Commits d3a6c0d (build) Ôćĺ faeeeb7 (cycle 1: deterministic archive/numbering, render hollow-guard, pipeline defense, probeÔćĺsonnet) Ôćĺ 4d9cca1 (cycle 2: promptÔćöparser format) Ôćĺ 6e09d8c (renderer ID-prefix hardening).**

This validates the orthogonal-validation contract: a fresh-context Workflow Red Team caught what an in-context "fixed it" pass would have missed (cycle 2 found the cycle-1 fix incomplete).

**Depth validation:** QA confirmed the design plausibly reproduces the Hilo reference depth ÔÇö the probe prompt actively pushes against the fixed-5 bias and toward feature-domain slicing (1-3 slices tiny Ôćĺ 15-40 large); the finder mandates enumerate-not-sample. Reference artifact `.gsd-t/m66-hilo-deep-scan-reference.md` (117 findings).

**Original definition (for history):** awaited the HiloAviation deep-scan output as the "deep enough" reference. User decisions (2026-05-29 17:57 PDT): run as a full milestone; wait for Hilo scan first; single verify pass per finding (not 3-vote).

**Origin / Regression report.** User ran `/gsd-t-scan` on HiloAviation (1,809 TS/TSX files, 361 pgTable defs, 151 route modules = 101 Hono + 50 Next API, 474 mvp-v2 components) and got a cursory **16-item** breadth register, where past scans on other projects went much deeper. Diagnosis (confirmed by reading `commands/gsd-t-scan.md` + repo state):

1. **Scan is the ONLY major phase never migrated to a native Workflow.** M61 created `templates/workflows/{execute,verify,wave,integrate,debug,quick,phase}.workflow.js` ÔÇö **no `gsd-t-scan.workflow.js`**. Scan is still 29KB of improvised prose.
2. **Fan-out is hard-coded to exactly 5 teammates (one per DIMENSION: architecture/business-rules/security/quality/contracts)** at `commands/gsd-t-scan.md:33,39,82,84-112`. **Zero volume scaling** ÔÇö a 5-file repo and a 1,809-file repo both get 5 agents. One `quality` sonnet agent is asked to cover dead-code+dup+complexity+errors+perf+naming+TODOs+test-gaps+deps across all 1,809 files in one context Ôćĺ it samples ~5 and stops. That IS the shallow register.
3. **Dead spawn references.** Scan cites `headless-default-contract.md` **v2.0.0** + `autoSpawnHeadless()` (lines 7,11,16) ÔÇö **neither exists in the repo** (M61/M65 orchestration-shell retirement removed them). So even the spawn path the prose describes is gone; it falls back to plain team-mode or a single improvised pass.

**Goal.** Migrate scan to a native volume-scaled Workflow so depth auto-scales with codebase volume on EVERY invocation ÔÇö no prompt improvisation.

**Planned shape (finalize at partition):**
- NEW `templates/workflows/gsd-t-scan.workflow.js`: (a) **volume-probe** stage (haiku) counts files/routes/tables/components per top-level area Ôćĺ derives a **slice list** (e.g. each of `src/lib/`'s 24 subdirs = 1 slice; ~15ÔÇô25 slices for Hilo, 1 for a tiny repo); (b) `pipeline()` per-slice **deep finder** (dimension-aware, mandate "enumerate every module, do NOT sample") Ôćĺ **single verify pass** per finding (user choice 2026-05-29: single verify, not 3-vote) confirming against real code, killing false positives; (c) `budget`-aware slice depth; (d) **synthesis** stage (opus) dedup/merge into `techdebt.md`, re-rank criticalÔćĺlow, continue TD numbering from archive. Keep deterministic `bin/scan-*.js` (schema/diagrams/HTML report) as stages.
- REWRITE `commands/gsd-t-scan.md` Ôćĺ thin `Workflow({scriptPath, args})` invoker matching the other 7; strip dead `autoSpawnHeadless`/`headless-default-contract v2.0.0` refs.
- Doc-ripple: `GSD-T-README.md`, `README.md`, `templates/CLAUDE-global.md`, `commands/gsd-t-help.md`, `package.json` (patch bump), progress decision-log.

**Validation target.** The HiloAviation deep scan (running now, separate folder, does NOT touch this repo) defines "deep enough". M66's new workflow must reproduce comparable depth automatically. BLOCKED until that artifact lands.

### M61 ÔÇö Platform Reconciliation (Native-First GSD-T) ÔÇö **PARTITIONED** (2026-05-29 11:46 PDT)

**Status: PARTITIONED ÔÇö 8 domains scoped under `.gsd-t/domains/m61-d{1-8}-*/`; `m61-integration-points.md` written; Wave 0 (v3.x-legacy branch) already DONE. Awaiting `/gsd-t-plan`. Baseline locked: bin/ = 37,785 LOC / 109 files at v3.29.11 (SC1 target ÔëĄ12,000 LOC).**

**Origin**: Opus 4.8 + current Claude Code (native 1M context, native background **Workflows** with deterministic pipeline/parallel/barriers/schema-validation/budget, native parallel agents, `/context`, `/usage`, Skills, comprehensive hooks, `/code-review ultra`) have absorbed the entire infrastructure layer GSD-T built across M34ÔÇôM54 to compensate for a 200K window + a runtime that couldn't spawn/background/relay. A maximal-native Workflow bake-off (2026-05-29) re-ran M58 as **one Workflow script** and reproduced every deterministic gate + both domains exactly ÔÇö AND its adversarial Red Team caught a live CRITICAL (Ôćĺ M60) that M58's in-context review missed. **Conclusion: the orchestration migration is both safe and strictly more reliable.**

**Goal**: Collapse GSD-T to its irreplaceable methodology layer riding on native primitives. Target: bin/ from ~38K LOC Ôćĺ ~8K LOC. **Net objective: most efficient, reliable, predictable build/rebuild/debug/deliver process** ÔÇö which means *less custom infra to maintain*, not more.

**Domains (pre-partition shape ÔÇö finalized at partition):**

- **D1 retire-context-runway** ÔÇö delete the context-meter / runway machinery now obsoleted by native 1M context + `/context` + native compaction: `token-budget.cjs`, `context-meter-config.cjs(+test)`, `context-budget-audit.cjs`, `runway-estimator.cjs`, `model-windows.cjs(+test)`, the context-meter PostToolUse hook, `.context-meter-state.json` plumbing. (~1,580 LOC + hook.)
- **D2 retire-unattended-relay** ÔÇö delete the cross-session relay supervisor now replaced by native background Workflows + `/loop`: `gsd-t-unattended.cjs(+.js dup)`, `-safety.cjs(+.js)`, `-platform.cjs(+.js)`, `-heartbeat.cjs`, `supervisor-pid-fingerprint.cjs`, `handoff-lock.cjs(+.js)`, `headless-auto-spawn.cjs(+.js)`, `check-headless-sessions.js`, `unattended-watch-format.cjs`, `gsd-t-worker-dispatch.cjs`, `gsd-t-orchestrator-recover.cjs` + the 3 `gsd-t-unattended*` commands. (~8,800 LOC ÔÇö largest demolition.)

(~4,100 LOC.)

(~2,000 LOC + scripts.)

(~6,500 LOC Ôćĺ ~500.)
- **D7 keep-and-reframe-validation** ÔÇö KEEP the methodology gates; reframe Red Team / QA / Design-Verify as **Workflow stages** (perspective-diverse adversarial `parallel()`), de-duped against native `/code-review ultra`. KEEP unchanged: `gsd-t-verify-gate(+judge)`, `gsd-t-ci-parity`, `gsd-t-build-coverage`, `gsd-t-test-data-ledger` (+ M60-hardened adapters), `journey-coverage(+cli)`, `cli-preflight`, `gsd-t-context-brief` (MORE valuable now ÔÇö cheap context for Workflow agents), `playwright-bootstrap`/`ui-detection`, scan engine, `rule-engine`, `graph-*`, `archive-progress`, `global-sync-manager`.
- **D8 doc-ripple-and-cockpit** ÔÇö rewrite CLAUDE-global/project + commandsÔćĺSkills mapping to drop retired-infra rules; **bake in the desktop-as-cockpit outcome** (see SC7).

**Falsifiable Success Criteria:**
- **SC1** ÔÇö bin/ LOC drops from ~38K to ÔëĄ ~12K (measured `wc -l` before/after); every deleted file proven to have zero live references first (safety scan).
- **SC2** ÔÇö a representative milestone (re-run of M58 or M52) completes end-to-end via the native-Workflow harness with all KEEP-list gates green and Red Team clean ÔÇö i.e., the bake-off result reproduces after the demolition.
- **SC3** ÔÇö zero regressions on the full unit suite vs. the M60 baseline (2466 pass / 1 known-flaky / 3 sqlite-skip), excluding tests deleted *with* their retired subject.
- **SC4** ÔÇö `gsd-t doctor` passes with no dangling references to retired modules; no command file references a deleted `bin/` script.
- **SC5** ÔÇö Red Team / QA / Design-Verify run as Workflow stages (not bespoke Task spawns), de-duped against `/code-review ultra` (no double-paying for correctness review).
- **SC6** ÔÇö every retired capability has a named native replacement documented in the milestone archive (retireÔćĺnative map), so nothing is lost silently (measure-don't-claim).
- **SC7 (desktop-as-cockpit)** ÔÇö after M61, **no routine build / rebuild / debug / deliver action requires the user to hand-type in a terminal**; the desktop app can drive all of it (orchestrate via Bash + Workflows + Skills). Verified by walking the full loop (partitionÔćĺplanÔćĺexecuteÔćĺverifyÔćĺdeliver) from the desktop on one real task. The only terminal-native residue allowed: background hooks (which run automatically, not user-initiated) and "must-outlive-app-close" overnight jobs.
- **SC8** ÔÇö Red Team GRUDGING PASS on the reconciled framework (adversarial Workflow pass finds no CRITICAL/HIGH in the migrated orchestration).

**Sequencing note (user directive, 2026-05-29)**: M61 is **initiated from the terminal CLI** ÔÇö it is the last big CLI-dependent job (editing/removing hooks, supervisor teardown, heavy git surgery on the very infra being removed). After M61 lands (SC7 verified), the user switches to the **desktop as single cockpit**.

**Pre-partition assessment**: large milestone ÔÇö 8 domains, mostly file-disjoint (each retire-domain owns its own bin files), but D6 (migrate) and D7/D8 (keep/reframe/doc) have ordering dependencies (migrate orchestration before deleting old orchestration; reframe validation before doc-ripple). Likely 3ÔÇô4 waves: retire-disjoint (D1ÔłąD3ÔłąD4ÔłąD5) Ôćĺ migrate (D6) Ôćĺ reframe+retire-relay (D7ÔłąD2) Ôćĺ doc+cockpit (D8). **Destructive Action Guard applies throughout** ÔÇö every deletion domain runs a zero-live-reference safety scan and pauses for approval before removing working functionality. Discussion phase recommended (this reshapes the framework's identity).

### M58 ÔÇö Test Data Cleanup Gate **COMPLETE** at v3.28.10 (2026-05-27). Origin: GSD-T-Board v0.1.10 ran `gsd-t-verify`, the Playwright suite passed, the milestone was tagged VERIFIED ÔÇö and 2442 `E2E_TEST_*` / `E2E_DRAG_*` ideas stayed live in the production data store. Root cause: GSD-T had no convention for tracking test data inserted during Verify and no purge step after the suite completes. **D1 test-data-ledger**: `bin/gsd-t-test-data-ledger.cjs` ships `{appendInsert, listInserts, purgeRunInserts, registerAdapter}` against an append-only JSONL ledger at `.gsd-t/test-data-ledger.jsonl`; 3 built-in adapters under `bin/gsd-t-test-data-adapters/` (`localStorage-key-prefix`, `file-json-array`, `sqlite-table-where`) each enforce a tagged-prefix guard as defense in depth; CLI `gsd-t test-data --list|--purge --run <id>` (exit 0/4/64). **D2 verify-cleanup-step + tagging convention**: `templates/test-helpers/test-data-fixture.ts` ships the Playwright `withTestData()` fixture (composes `{PREFIX}_{runId}_{counter}` IDs, calls `appendInsert` on `register`, opt-in `purgePerTest`); `commands/gsd-t-verify.md` Step 4.5 runs `gsd-t test-data --purge` after E2E + before VERDICT, FAILs verify on adapter errors. **SCs**: 7/7 PASS ÔÇö ledger records 5 inserts, purge removes them and reports `purged.length===5`, planted adapter throw lands in `errors[]` (FAIL decision), clean E2E reports `purged=5 skipped=0 errors=0`, **2649/2649 tests pass (zero regressions; baseline was 2587)**, Red Team **6/6 attacks defended** (untagged-id reject, tag-prefix-tamper reject, unknown-adapter structured error, SQL-injection reject, no stray writes, bad-adapter-return-value caught), doc-ripple complete. **Contracts**: `test-data-ledger-contract.md` v1.0.0 STABLE + `test-data-tagging-contract.md` v1.0.0 STABLE. **Versioning**: minor bump 3.27.10 Ôćĺ 3.28.10 (new feature, additive).

- 2026-06-22 12:32 PDT: [m90][VERIFY Ôćĺ 6th FAIL Ôćĺ HALT + ESCALATE design fork] 6th verify = VERIFY-FAILED. **The loop-ledger STATE MODEL is now FIXED ÔÇö the fix held:** code-review dropped to 4 NITS (zero important), QA GREEN (1987/0, 0 shallow), and NO finding hits the cumulative-counter/reset state model. But the Red Team found a genuine LOGICAL BIND I created: **R-FAIL-3 is now VACUOUS** ÔÇö the debug workflow calls `record-re-examination` the INSTANT it detects run-local non-convergence (line 388Ôćĺ399), so by the time verify reads the state it's always clean Ôćĺ the gate can never fire on a real non-converging loop. **This is the direct conflict between the two requirements: fix-cycle-2's "auto-reset so a halt doesn't permanently brick future verifies" vs. R-FAIL-3's "FAIL when there's an unresolved halt." - 2026-06-21 15:55 PDT: [m89][PAUSE + re-scope][backlog #38/#39] User paused M89 at verify (after 8 verify cycles, all converging on the silent-miss class) and RE-SCOPED. Two insights: (1) **M89 is too narrow.** Its "guessing" framing only covered FACTUAL assumptions ("do I know what the code/API says?"). The user named the dangerous omission: the system also assumes an APPROACH/architecture is correct without proof ("I'll fix it this way"; "the existing code was written right, build on it") and PLOWS FORWARD on the unproven approach ÔÇö the root of binvoice's whack-a-mole + the M87 (7-cycle) and M89 (8-cycle) plan/verify loops (each cycle a new "right fix" on a wrong premise). The real feature = the UNPROVEN-ASSUMPTION doctrine: any unproven assumption (factual OR architectural) Ôćĺ STOP Ôćĺ research how others solved it Ôćĺ re-examine the premise Ôćĺ then proceed. Backlogged #38 (HIGHEST leverage; M89's external-fact auto-research becomes its factual slice). The trigger of the re-scope: M89's classifier recognized "external" via a hardcoded ~40-vendor list ÔÇö a frozen belief for an OPEN set; any out-of-list vendor (GitHub/Slack/OpenAI) silently routed internal Ôćĺ the exact silent-miss M89 exists to prevent. Lesson: never hardcode a finite list for an open category; mechanical layer knows only CLOSED sets (own repo files), LLM judges the open world. (2) **Red Team has no realism/scope gate** ÔÇö escalates unlikely/contrived edge cases to CRITICAL with equal weight to real money/security bugs. User's design (banked #39): a separate Realism agent the Red Team argues scope with (2 attempts, 2 rejections Ôćĺ documented deferred-out-of-scope); + my refinements: Realism rules only on scope-not-validity with a HARD FLOOR (money/security/data-loss/silent-wrong-output always in-scope), deferral-with-ledger not dismissal.
